      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n28287-2" target="عَدِيدٌ" n="2" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n28290"/></foreign> is syn. therewith [in this sense, as will be seen in what follows]; (A;) <hi rend="ital">a quantity composed of units;</hi> and therefore not [properly] applicable to one; but accord. to the grammarians, one belongs to the predicament of<foreign lang="ar">العَدَدُ</foreign> because it is the root thereof, and because it implies quantity, for when it is said “ How many hast thou? ” it is as proper to answer “ One ” as it is to answer “ Three ” &amp;c.: (Msb:) pl. <foreign lang="ar">أَعْدَادٌ</foreign>.                      <L>
                        <foreign lang="ar">إِذَا مَا قَارَنَ القَمَرُ الثُّرَيَّا</foreign>
                     </L> 
                     <L>
                        <foreign lang="ar">لِثَالِثَةِ فَقَدْ ذَهَبَ الشِّتَآءُ</foreign>
                     </L> 
                  </quote> [<hi rend="ital">When the moon is in conjunction with the Pleiades in a third</hi> night, <hi rend="ital">then winter has departed</hi>], AHeyth said, [as though what was the case at a particular period of a cycle were the case generally,] the moon is in conjunction with <foreign lang="ar">الثريّا</foreign> only in a third night from the new moon, [meaning only once in the year in the third night,] and that is in the beginning of spring and the end of winter. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="7">-b7-</sense>  And <foreign lang="ar">عِدَادٌ</foreign> and

                  <hi rend="ital">The pain of the venomous sting,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">bite, returned to him with vehemence at the expiration of a year.</hi> (S, O, * K.) And <foreign lang="ar">بِهِ</foreign>
